# <a name="obsolete-types-in-the-net-framework"></a><span data-ttu-id="d8b1a-102">Tipi obsoleti in .NET Framework</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d8b1a-102">Obsolete Types in the .NET Framework</span></span>
<a name="introduction"></a> <span data-ttu-id="d8b1a-103">Le tabelle in questo articolo elencano i tipi obsoleti in [!INCLUDE[net_v45](../../../includes/net-v45-md.md)] e [!INCLUDE[net_v46](../../../includes/net-v46-md.md)], organizzati per assembly.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d8b1a-103">The tables in this article list the types that are obsolete in the [!INCLUDE[net_v45](../../../includes/net-v45-md.md)] and the [!INCLUDE[net_v46](../../../includes/net-v46-md.md)], organized by assembly.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d8b1a-104">Usare i seguenti collegamenti per vedere un elenco di tipi obsoleti e le alternative consigliate in ogni assembly.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d8b1a-104">Use the following links to see a list of the obsolete types and the recommended alternatives in each assembly.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d8b1a-105">Poiché questi tipi sono obsoleti, lo sono anche tutti i relativi membri.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d8b1a-105">Because these types are obsolete, all their members are also obsolete.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d8b1a-106">Per un elenco di altri membri obsoleti nella libreria di classi .NET Framework, vedere [Membri obsoleti](../../../docs/framework/whats-new/obsolete-members.md).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d8b1a-106">For a list of additional obsolete members in the .NET Framework class library, see [Obsolete Members](../../../docs/framework/whats-new/obsolete-members.md).</span></span>
